name:L‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçc‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äçe‚Äçr‚Äç ‚ÄçM‚Äça‚Äçn
info:1 King Bed Park View
info:Stayed in September 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:56 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 11, 2021
msg:Park Hyatt Guangzhou is a truly unique hotel. While other top-end hotels chase after grandness, sophistication, and luxuriousness, Park Hyatt keeps up its pursuit for simplicity and nature and performs them in a magically elegant fashion. It is a hotel as fresh as a deep tranquil bamboo forest, where the only sound one can hear comes from the wind.

Such emphasis on simplicity and nature is well manifested in its rooms. Park Hyatt Guangzhou substantially utilizes plain wooden furniture ‚Äì from its mini-bar cardboard, desk, bedside table, to its floor. The furniture is so simple to the extent that I would not be surprised if someone told me they come from the village house of a grassroots family in rural Hunan. However, it is on these simple items that Park Hyatt Guangzhou plays its magic. The hotel hosts these pieces of furniture on top of a plain but exquisite background, thus extracting the simple beauty inside them while cleaning all their humble elements away. That is why I would say that the interior design of Park Hyatt Guangzhou is really an art masterpiece. It is easy to design a lovely room by using luxurious materials, but it requires a master to create something adorable by using humble items, and Park Hyatt Guangzhou does just that. Because of so, the vibe of Park Hyatt Guangzhou is the most unique among all the top-end hotels in Guangzhou, which all opt for the easier route of luxuriousness. It is because of this that I would also say that Park Hyatt Guangzhou is the hotel that can calm one‚Äôs mind the most in Guangzhou. I said that Grand Hyatt Shenzhen is like an oasis in a bustling town; now, I would say that Park Hyatt Guangzhou is even more than that ‚Äì it is an Alps forest in the most premium land of southern China.

The people at Park Hyatt Guangzhou are so as well. Every lady and gentleman I had the honor to encounter at Park Hyatt Guangzhou diffused out a great sense of peace and calm. Usually, this is not an ideal quality for hotel people because it means the lack of enthusiasm when communicating with their guests. However, it is not the case in Park Hyatt Guangzhou. While sending out enormous peace and calm, the ladies and gentlemen at Park Hyatt Guangzhou could still all make me feel incredibly warm and cared for. If this is not magic, what is magic? It is especially so with Ms. Beryl Tang, who helped me change my room without any hesitation even when it was already midnight. Beyond that, Beryl even personally guided me to visit different rooms and informed me about the characteristics of each room in a manner that could not be more friendly and genuine. Our exchange was short because of your efficiency but I really enjoyed it, Beryl. It really surprised me when I realized that it was still your internship. I had never imagined that such a young lady would be able to deliver such professional services, which were professional to the extent that I thought you already had many years of experience in the industry! I firmly believe you will soon become a superstar in the hotel industry, Beryl! Thanks for everything.

msg:Regrettable accommodation experience, hope it can be improved

I'm sorry to say that my experience at the Park Hyatt Guangzhou fell far short of my expectations. I had several issues that I feel should not be happening for a hotel with such a reputation.

First, there seemed to be a problem with the room's air conditioning system, which prevented it from cooling properly. Considering Guangzhou's climate, a well-working air conditioning system is essential. However, in my room, the air conditioner never seemed to provide enough cooling no matter how I adjusted it, which made my night's sleep very uncomfortable.

Secondly, I was quite disappointed with the quality of the beds. The bed was so hard that you could visibly feel the springs underneath it, providing a very cheap and uncomfortable sleeping experience. This is an extremely rare experience for me in an upscale hotel and far from the standard I've come to expect from a Park Hyatt.

In addition, I am not satisfied with the breakfast service. Breakfast was advertised until 10am, but when I arrived at 9:40, there was a long line of customers waiting. Even more dissatisfying is that the front desk staff did not seem to care about the needs of the guests. No one came to ask or guide where to wait in line, and no one informed them of possible waiting times. This lack of efficiency and customer care is unacceptable under any circumstances.

Overall, my stay fell short of expectations in many important aspects, which is really disappointing for a Park Hyatt hotel that symbolizes high-quality service and facilities. I hope the hotel will take this feedback seriously and make improvements where necessary to ensure that future guests can enjoy the comfort and satisfaction they deserve.

1-Location: Not much difference, K11 is downstairs in Rosewood, and Friendship Store is next to Park Hyatt.
2-Parking: The difference is not much, and the road for Rosewood to enter the parking lot is narrow. Park Hyatt has mechanical bits.
3- Hygiene: Park Hyatt wins. In response to these two stays, the magnificent bathtub has hair, the indoor bathroom and the sliding door in the middle of the room have residual appetite, the carpet has broken bread, and the work table has broken appetite, and the sanitary condition is appalling. Park Hyatt hygiene is acceptable.
4- Warm feeling: Park Hyatt wins. Both houses have fruit, but Park Hyatt has a disinfection kit. This time, the children in Park Hyatt snorted in the swimming pool, and the housekeeping quickly provided iodophors and Band-Aids. The decoration of the lobby and rooms, the aroma of aroma, Park Hyatt is more comfortable.
5-Scenery: Magnificent High, the last time I lived was on the 90th floor, and the Park Hyatt was on the 56th floor, I feel the same. Magnificent has a slight advantage.
6- Wellness Center: Park Hyatt wins. The treadmill has an isolation glass, which is very considerate. Park Hyatt has a waiter who regularly sprays and wipes it for disinfection. The Park Hyatt locker room has a large hot tub with massage and wet steam. Pool view is good. Rosewood is more like an apar**ent facility.
7-Service: I think Park Hyatt is better, although everyone is polite, but Park Hyatt feels more natural service regardless of catering, housekeeping, fitness or front desk. Catering is also a coaxing attitude.
8- Epidemic prevention: Park Hyatt wins. The Park Hyatt parking lot needs to scan the code, the main entrance needs to scan the code, the front desk needs to see the itinerary code, and the fitness center needs to make an appoin**ent to prevent the number of guests from exceeding a certain number. The rooms are equipped with masks and disinfectants, which are very comfortable and safe. The Rosewood parking lot has QR code scanning, but it is not available after arrival, and there are no supporting anti-epidemic materials.
9- Bathroom: Leveling. Park Hyatt has an electric toilet, but the water pressure is average. The magnificent shower was comfortable and the bathtub drained smoothly. The matching cleaning supplies are about the same.
10- Room comfort: Park Hyatt wins. Although the Park Hyatt rooms are not magnificent, they are reasonably furnished. The carpet design is more reasonable and safer than the magnificent ones. The Park Hyatt central air conditioner is more comfortable than the magnificent ones.
11- Value for money. Magnificent 1600, Park Hyatt 1200, I chose the cheapest room type, Park Hyatt wins.

At night, the Guangzhou Tower is amazed by the ever-changing colors. Swimming on the 65th floor seems to be connected to the sky, overlooking the slow flowing of the Pearl River, the boats on the river, and the grassy meadows on the river bank.
